# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-102">Veraltete Member in .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-103">In den Tabellen in diesem Artikel werden die Typmember nach Assembly geordnet aufgeführt, die in .NET Framework 4.5 und höheren Versionen veraltet sind.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-104">Über die nachfolgenden Links finden Sie eine Liste der veralteten Member und empfohlenen Alternativen in den jeweiligen Assemblys.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-105">In diesem Thema werden nicht die Member veralteter Typen aufgeführt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-105">This topic doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-106">Eine Liste veralteter Typen finden Sie unter [Veraltete Typen](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete Types](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

<a name="SystemMembers"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-140">Veraltete Member in Systemassemblys</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-141">In den folgenden Tabellen sind die veralteten Member in Systemassemblys aufgeführt.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a3ccc-142">Diese Assemblys werden zur allgemeinen Anwendungsentwicklung für .NET Framework verwendet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a3ccc-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
